 sena ke uttari cmand, jiskaa mukhyalay udhampur he, ke pravaktaa karnal es

 goswami ne bataaya, 'siachin main laapata javaanon kii talash puri ho gai he
 The credit for this goes to the determination of the rescue team, who managed to get Lance Nayak Hanumanthappa Koppad alive within 30 feet of snow even in extreme conditions
 'tippaniyan Colonel Goswami said, 'lance Nayak Hanumanthappa Kopper has demonstrated his supernatural ability to survive alive even after being buried under snow for 6 days

 This tracking will be based on IMEI number, that is, even if the thief has removed the SIM from your smartphone, it can still be tracked and its service can be blocked

 is par kaam july 2017 se chal rahaa he
 For setting up CEIR in the country, the government has proposed to pay an amount of Rs 15 crore so that mobile phone theft can be curbed
 CEIR system ke tahat chori kiye gaye mobile phone kii sabhi sarvice block kar di jaaengi
 Even if the SIM card is removed from the stolen mobile phone and the SIM of another network is installed, then this technology will work and all the services of that mobile phone can be blocked
